var vsCFTagsNonEuFunctions = vsCFTagsNonEuFunctions || [];

vsCFExecuteEuTags();
vsCFExecuteNonEuTags();

//Execute Eu Tags Function
function vsCFExecuteEuTags() {
        for (f of vsCFTagsEUFunctions) {
                f();
        }

        vsCFTagsEUFunctions = [];
}

//Execute None Eu Tags Function
function vsCFExecuteNonEuTags() {
        for (f of vsCFTagsNonEuFunctions) {
                f();

}

function vsQueueAd(adunit) {
    function vsEUAdUnit() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
            googletag.display(adunit); 
    });
    }
    function vsNonEUAdUnit() {
        googletag.cmd.push(function() { 
        if (window.deployads) {
        deployads.push(function() {
            deployads.gpt.display(adunit); 
            });
        } else {
            googletag.display(adunit); 
        }
        });
    }
    vsCFTagsEUFunctions.push(vsEUAdUnit);
    vsCFTagsNonEuFunctions.push(vsNonEUAdUnit);
}

        adProviders: gfAllFcPartners,
        isAdProviderAllowed: function( providerName ) {
                if(
                        !providerName
                        || typeof googlefc === 'undefined'
                        || typeof googlefc.getConsentedProviderIds === 'undefined'
                        //|| googleprivacySettings.trackUserOk === false
                ) {
                        return false;
                }
                // get google FC Consented provider Ids for the current site

        }
};

					el.parentNode.insertBefore(s, el);
				})();
			}
		});

		console.log("cf: comscore googlefc not found.");
	}
}

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function vsCFViglinkEU() {
	if (typeof googlefc == "object") {
		googlefc.callbackQueue.push(function() {
			if ( gfchelper.isAdProviderAllowed("viglink") ) {
				vglnk = {key: '5e5e6e04e939b9674c384ca8b03117f4'};
				(function(d, t) {
					var s = d.createElement(t);
						s.type = 'text/javascript';
						s.async = true;
						s.src = 'https://cdn.viglink.com/api/vglnk.js';
					var r = d.getElementsByTagName(t)[0];
						r.parentNode.insertBefore(s, r);
				}(document, 'script'));
			}
		});
	} else { 
		console.log("cf: viglink googlefc not found.");
	}
}
function vsCFViglinkNonEU() {
	vglnk = {key: '5e5e6e04e939b9674c384ca8b03117f4'};
    (function(d, t) {
        var s = d.createElement(t);
            s.type = 'text/javascript';
            s.async = true;
            s.src = 'https://cdn.viglink.com/api/vglnk.js';
        var r = d.getElementsByTagName(t)[0];
            r.parentNode.insertBefore(s, r);
    }(document, 'script'));
}

//Add viglink tag functions to eu and non-eu arrays.
vsCFTagsEUFunctions.push(vsCFViglinkEU);
vsCFTagsNonEuFunctions.push(vsCFViglinkNonEU);

  <!-- Adblock Check -->
  <div class="afs_ads">
  </div>
  <script>
   (function() {
    var adBlockDetector = function() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            if (!document.getElementsByClassName) return;
            
            var ads = document.getElementsByClassName("afs_ads");
            ad  = ads[ads.length - 1];

            if (!ad || ad.innerHTML.length == 0 || ad.clientHeight === 0) {
                _gaq.push(["_trackEvent", "Adblock", "Blocked", "true",,true]);
            } else {
                ad.style.display = "none";
                _gaq.push(["_trackEvent", "Adblock", "Unblocked", "false",,true]);
            }

        }, 500);
    }

    /* Attach a listener for page load */
    if (window.addEventListener) {
        window.addEventListener("load", adBlockDetector, false);
    } else {
        window.attachEvent("onload", adBlockDetector); //IE
    }
})();
  </script>
  <!-- /Adblock Check-->
